; this file is to store all static SQL statements used in our system
; all table names in the SQL statement should be in lower case
; all the SQL statements store in this file follows a format like
; [table name]
; ID=SQL Statement (if the statment too long, separate it using '+' as its first character in the newline)
; [[common]] 
; contains all the statements which can use by all the database system that we currently supported in our system
; [[Oracle]]
; contains the statements which can only apply in Oracle database
; [[MySQL]]
; contains the statements which can only apply in MySQL database

[AlarmState]
; the following SQL Statements of the AlarmRule table used in source file: 
; AlarmStateAccessFactory.cpp
[[common]]
ALARMSTATE_SELECT_71001=SELECT Pkey,Name, DisplayName, TypeKey FROM AlarmState

[System]
; the following SQL Statements of the AlarmRule table used in source file: 
; SystemAccessFactory.cpp
[[common]]
SYSTEM_SELECT_72001=SELECT Pkey,name, is_physical,exclusive_control FROM System

[AlarmRule]
; the following SQL Statements of the AlarmRule table used in source file: 
; AlarmRuleAccessFactory.cpp, AlarmRuleHelper.cpp, SuppressionRuleHelper.cpp
[[common]]
ALARMRULE_SELECT_1001=SELECT pkey, ruleType FROM alarmrule
ALARMRULE_SELECT_1002=SELECT pkey FROM alarmrule WHERE ruleType = '%s'
ALARMRULE_SELECT_1003=SELECT a.pkey FROM alarmrule a, entity e WHERE a.ruleType = '%s' AND a.entitykey = e.pkey AND e.locationkey = %s
ALARMRULE_SELECT_1004=SELECT pkey FROM alarmrule WHERE ruletype = 'MMS' and alarmtype = %s
ALARMRULE_SELECT_1005=SELECT pkey FROM alarmrule WHERE ruleType = '%s' AND entityKey IN (SELECT pkey FROM entity WHERE locationKey = %s)
ALARMRULE_SELECT_1006=SELECT pkey FROM alarmrule WHERE ruleType = '%s' AND entityKey IN (SELECT pkey FROM entity WHERE locationKey = 
    + (SELECT pkey FROM location WHERE name = '%s'))
ALARMRULE_SELECT_1007=SELECT ruleType FROM alarmrule WHERE pkey = %s
ALARMRULE_SELECT_1008=SELECT pkey from alarmrule WHERE entitytypekey = %s AND entitykey = %s AND rule_trigger = '%s' AND ruletype = '%s' AND %s
ALARMRULE_UPDATE_1151=UPDATE alarmrule SET entityTypeKey = %s, entityKey = %s, %s rule_trigger = '%s', ruleType = '%s' %s 
ALARMRULE_INSERT_1301=INSERT INTO alarmrule (pkey, entitytypekey, entitykey, alarmtype, rule_trigger, ruletype %s) VALUES (%s, %s, %s, %s '%s', '%s' %s)
ALARMRULE_DELETE_1401=DELETE FROM alarmrule WHERE pkey = %s
[[Oracle]]
ALARMRULE_SELECT_1051=SELECT ALARMRULE_SEQ.NEXTVAL FROM Dual
ALARMRULE_SELECT_1052=SELECT TO_CHAR(DATE_CREATED,'YYYYMMDDHH24MISS') from alarmrule where pkey = %s
ALARMRULE_SELECT_1053=SELECT TO_CHAR(DATE_CREATED,'YYYYMMDDHH24MISS'), TO_CHAR(DATE_MODIFIED,'YYYYMMDDHH24MISS') from alarmrule where pkey = %s
ALARMRULE_SELECT_1054=SELECT entitytypekey, entitykey, nvl(alarmtype, 0) as ALARM_TYPE, rule_trigger, ruletype, alarmdescription, nvl(created_by_session_key, ' ') 
    + as CREATED_BY_SESSION_KEY, nvl(created_by_Profile_key, 0) as CREATED_BY_PROFILE_KEY, nvl(created_by_Operator_Name, ' ') as CREATED_BY_OPERATOR_NAME, TO_CHAR(DATE_MODIFIED,'YYYYMMDDHH24MISS'), TO_CHAR(DATE_CREATED,'YYYYMMDDHH24MISS') FROM alarmrule WHERE pkey = %s
[[MySQL]]
ALARMRULE_SELECT_1051=SELECT func_seq_get_next_number('alarmrule_seq')
ALARMRULE_SELECT_1052=SELECT DATE_FORMAT(DATE_CREATED,'%%Y%%m%%d%%H%%i%%S') from alarmrule where pkey = %s
ALARMRULE_SELECT_1053=SELECT DATE_FORMAT(DATE_CREATED,'%%Y%%m%%d%%H%%i%%S'), DATE_FORMAT(DATE_MODIFIED,'%%Y%%m%%d%%H%%i%%S') from alarmrule where pkey = %s
ALARMRULE_SELECT_1054=SELECT entitytypekey, entitykey, IF(alarmtype IS NULL, 0, alarmtype) as ALARM_TYPE, rule_trigger, ruletype, alarmdescription,  
    + IF(created_by_session_key IS NULL or created_by_session_key = '', ' ', created_by_session_key) as CREATED_BY_SESSION_KEY, 
	+ IF(created_by_Profile_key IS NULL , 0, created_by_Profile_key) as CREATED_BY_PROFILE_KEY,
	+ IF(created_by_Operator_Name IS NULL or created_by_Operator_Name = '', ' ', created_by_Operator_Name) as CREATED_BY_OPERATOR_NAME, DATE_FORMAT(DATE_MODIFIED,'%%Y%%m%%d%%H%%i%%S'), 
    + DATE_FORMAT(DATE_CREATED,'%%Y%%m%%d%%H%%i%%S') FROM alarmrule WHERE pkey = %s

ME_ALARM_TYPE_SELECT_1501=select meatyp_id from me_alarm_type where type_name = '%s'
ME_ALARM_TYPE_UPDATE_1651=update me_alarm_type set type_name = '%s', type_description = '%s', measev_id = %s, print_alarm = %s, system_alarm = %s, persist_alarm = %s, alarm_value = '%s', normal_value = '%s', mms_state = %s where meatyp_id = %s
ME_ALARM_TYPE_DELETE_1901=delete from me_alarm_type where meatyp_id = %s
[[Oracle]]
ME_ALARM_TYPE_SELECT_1551=select a.meatyp_id, a.type_name, a.memcon_id, mc.context_name, nvl(a.type_description,'NULL') as type_description,
    + a.measev_id, a.print_alarm, a.system_alarm, a.isvisible, a.persist_alarm, a.alarm_value, a.normal_value, a.mms_state,
    + TO_CHAR(a.date_modified,'YYYYMMDDHH24MISS'), TO_CHAR(a.date_created,'YYYYMMDDHH24MISS'), a.physical_alarm from me_alarm_type a,
    + me_message_context mc where a.memcon_id = mc.memcon_id and a.meatyp_id = %s
ME_ALARM_TYPE_SELECT_1552=select a.meatyp_id, a.type_name, a.memcon_id, mc.context_name, nvl(a.type_description,'NULL') as type_description,
    + a.measev_id, a.print_alarm, a.system_alarm, a.isvisible, a.persist_alarm, a.alarm_value, a.normal_value, a.mms_state,
    + TO_CHAR(a.date_modified,'YYYYMMDDHH24MISS'), TO_CHAR(a.date_created,'YYYYMMDDHH24MISS'), a.physical_alarm from me_alarm_type a,
    + me_message_context mc where a.memcon_id = mc.memcon_id and a.type_name = '%s'
ME_ALARM_TYPE_SELECT_1553=select a.meatyp_id, a.type_name, a.memcon_id, mc.context_name, nvl(a.type_description,'NULL') as type_description, 
    + a.measev_id, a.print_alarm, a.system_alarm, a.isvisible, a.persist_alarm, a.alarm_value, a.normal_value, a.mms_state,
    + TO_CHAR(a.date_modified,'YYYYMMDDHH24MISS'), TO_CHAR(a.date_created,'YYYYMMDDHH24MISS') , a.physical_alarm from me_alarm_type a, 
    + me_message_context mc where a.memcon_id = mc.memcon_id and a.isvisible = 1 order by a.meatyp_id asc
ME_ALARM_TYPE_SELECT_1554=select a.meatyp_id, a.type_name, a.memcon_id, mc.context_name, nvl(a.type_description,'NULL') as type_description, 
    + a.measev_id, a.print_alarm, a.system_alarm, a.isvisible, a.persist_alarm, a.alarm_value, a.normal_value, a.mms_state,
    + TO_CHAR(a.date_modified,'YYYYMMDDHH24MISS'), TO_CHAR(a.date_created,'YYYYMMDDHH24MISS'), a.physical_alarm from me_alarm_type a, 
    + me_message_context mc where a.memcon_id = mc.memcon_id and a.isvisible = 1
ME_ALARM_TYPE_SELECT_1555=select a.meatyp_id, a.type_name, a.memcon_id, mc.context_name, nvl(a.type_description,'NULL') as type_description, a.measev_id, a.print_alarm, a.system_alarm, a.isvisible,
    + a.persist_alarm, a.alarm_value, a.normal_value, a.mms_state, TO_CHAR(a.date_modified,'YYYYMMDDHH24MISS'), TO_CHAR(a.date_created,'YYYYMMDDHH24MISS'), a.physical_alarm from 
    + me_alarm_type a, me_message_context mc where a.memcon_id = mc.memcon_id and a.meatyp_id = %s
[[MySQL]]
ME_ALARM_TYPE_SELECT_1551=select a.meatyp_id, a.type_name, a.memcon_id, mc.context_name, IF(a.type_description IS NULL or a.type_description = '', 'NULL', a.type_description) as type_description,
    + a.measev_id, a.print_alarm, a.system_alarm, a.isvisible, a.persist_alarm, a.alarm_value, a.normal_value, a.mms_state,

    + me_message_context mc where a.memcon_id = mc.memcon_id and a.meatyp_id = %s
ME_ALARM_TYPE_SELECT_1552=select a.meatyp_id, a.type_name, a.memcon_id, mc.context_name, IF(a.type_description IS NULL or a.type_description = '', 'NULL', a.type_description) as type_description,
    + a.measev_id, a.print_alarm, a.system_alarm, a.isvisible, a.persist_alarm, a.alarm_value, a.normal_value, a.mms_state,
    + DATE_FORMAT(a.date_modified, '%%Y%%m%%d%%H%%i%%S'), DATE_FORMAT(a.date_created,'%%Y%%m%%d%%H%%i%%S'), a.physical_alarm from me_alarm_type a,
    + me_message_context mc where a.memcon_id = mc.memcon_id and a.type_name = '%s'
ME_ALARM_TYPE_SELECT_1553=select a.meatyp_id, a.type_name, a.memcon_id, mc.context_name, IF(a.type_description IS NULL or a.type_description = '', 'NULL', a.type_description) as type_description, 
    + a.measev_id, a.print_alarm, a.system_alarm, a.isvisible, a.persist_alarm, a.alarm_value, a.normal_value, a.mms_state,
    + DATE_FORMAT(a.date_modified, '%Y%m%d%H%i%S'), DATE_FORMAT(a.date_created,'%Y%m%d%H%i%S'), a.physical_alarm from me_alarm_type a, 
    + me_message_context mc where a.memcon_id = mc.memcon_id and a.isvisible = 1 order by a.meatyp_id asc
ME_ALARM_TYPE_SELECT_1554=select a.meatyp_id, a.type_name, a.memcon_id, mc.context_name, IF(a.type_description IS NULL or a.type_description = '', 'NULL', a.type_description) as type_description,

ME_ALARM_TYPE_SELECT_1555=select a.meatyp_id, a.type_name, a.memcon_id, mc.context_name, IF(a.type_description IS NULL or a.type_description = '','NULL',a.type_description) as type_description, a.measev_id, a.print_alarm, a.system_alarm, a.isvisible,
    + a.persist_alarm, a.alarm_value, a.normal_value, a.mms_state, DATE_FORMAT(a.date_modified,'%%Y%%m%%d%%H%%i%%S'), DATE_FORMAT(a.date_created,'%%Y%%m%%d%%H%%i%%S'), a.physical_alarm from

[ALARMPLANMAPS]
; the following SQL Statements of the ALARMPLANMAPS table used in source file: 
; AlarmPlanAssocAccessFactory.cpp,AlarmPlanAssocHelper.cpp,IncidentReportHelper.cpp
[[common]]
ALARMPLANMAPS_SELECT_2001=SELECT alarmplanmaps1.planpath AS PLAN_ID FROM alarmplanmaps alarmplanmaps1, alarm alarm1, entity entity1 WHERE ((alarmplanmaps1.entitykey = alarm1.entitykey	AND alarm1.TYPE = alarmplanmaps1.alarmtypekey)
    + OR (alarmplanmaps1.entitytypekey = entity1.typekey AND alarm1.TYPE = alarmplanmaps1.alarmtypekey)) AND alarm1.alarm_id = '%s' AND entity1.pkey = alarm1.entitykey UNION
    + SELECT ae_alarm_rule_param1.action_parameter_value AS PLAN_ID FROM alarmrule alarmrule1,alarm alarm1,ae_alarm_rule_param ae_alarm_rule_param1,entity entity1
    + WHERE ((alarmrule1.entitykey = alarm1.entitykey AND alarm1.TYPE = alarmrule1.alarmtype) OR (alarmrule1.entitytypekey = entity1.typekey AND alarm1.TYPE = alarmrule1.alarmtype))
    + AND ae_alarm_rule_param1.alarm_rule_key = alarmrule1.pkey AND ae_alarm_rule_param1.action_parameter_type = 'PLAN_PATH' AND alarm1.alarm_id = '%s' AND entity1.pkey = alarm1.entitykey
ALARMPLANMAPS_UPDATE_2151=update alarmplanmaps set ENTITYKEY = %s,ENTITYTYPEKEY = %s,ALARMTYPEKEY = %s,PLANPATH = '%s'  where pkey = %s
ALARMPLANMAPS_INSERT_2301=insert into alarmplanmaps (PKEY,ENTITYTYPEKEY,ENTITYKEY,ALARMTYPEKEY,PLANPATH) values (%s, %s, %s, %s, '%s')
ALARMPLANMAPS_DELETE_2401=delete from alarmplanmaps where pkey = %s
[[Oracle]]
ALARMPLANMAPS_SELECT_2051=select PKEY, ENTITYTYPEKEY, ENTITYKEY, PLANPATH, ALARMTYPEKEY, TO_CHAR(DATE_MODIFIED,'YYYYMMDDHH24MISS'), TO_CHAR(DATE_CREATED,'YYYYMMDDHH24MISS') from alarmplanmaps
ALARMPLANMAPS_SELECT_2052=select PKEY, ENTITYTYPEKEY, ENTITYKEY, PLANPATH, ALARMTYPEKEY, TO_CHAR(DATE_MODIFIED,'YYYYMMDDHH24MISS'), TO_CHAR(DATE_CREATED,'YYYYMMDDHH24MISS') from alarmplanmaps WHERE pkey = %s
ALARMPLANMAPS_SELECT_2053=select ALARMPLANMAPS_SEQ.NEXTVAL from DUAL
ALARMPLANMAPS_SELECT_2054=select TO_CHAR(DATE_CREATED,'YYYYMMDDHH24MISS') from alarmplanmaps where PKEY = %s
ALARMPLANMAPS_SELECT_2055=select TO_CHAR(DATE_CREATED,'YYYYMMDDHH24MISS'), TO_CHAR(DATE_MODIFIED,'YYYYMMDDHH24MISS') from alarmplanmaps where PKEY = %s
[[MySQL]]
ALARMPLANMAPS_SELECT_2051=select PKEY, ENTITYTYPEKEY, ENTITYKEY, PLANPATH, ALARMTYPEKEY, DATE_FORMAT(DATE_MODIFIED,'%Y%m%d%H%i%S'), DATE_FORMAT(DATE_CREATED,'%Y%m%d%H%i%S') from alarmplanmaps
ALARMPLANMAPS_SELECT_2052=select PKEY, ENTITYTYPEKEY, ENTITYKEY, PLANPATH, ALARMTYPEKEY, DATE_FORMAT(DATE_MODIFIED,'%%Y%%m%%d%%H%%i%%S'), DATE_FORMAT(DATE_CREATED,'%%Y%%m%%d%%H%%i%%S') from alarmplanmaps WHERE pkey = %s
ALARMPLANMAPS_SELECT_2053=select func_seq_get_next_number('ALARMPLANMAPS_SEQ')
ALARMPLANMAPS_SELECT_2054=select DATE_FORMAT(DATE_CREATED,'%%Y%%m%%d%%H%%i%%S') from alarmplanmaps where PKEY = %s
ALARMPLANMAPS_SELECT_2055=select DATE_FORMAT(DATE_CREATED,'%%Y%%m%%d%%H%%i%%S'), DATE_FORMAT(DATE_MODIFIED,'%%Y%%m%%d%%H%%i%%S') from alarmplanmaps where PKEY = %s

[entity_v]
; the following SQL Statements of the Entity table used in source file: 
; some of the standard SQL statement will be change to directly using the entity table to improve the performance
; EntityAccessFactory.cpp, EntityHelper.cpp, ConfigEntity.cpp TisConfigAccess.cpp
[[common]]
ENTITY_V_SELECT_2501=select e.pkey, e.name, a.name, e.locationkey from entity e, entity a where upper(e.name) = upper('%s') and a.pkey = e.agentkey and 
    + e.deleted = 0 and a.deleted = 0
ENTITY_V_SELECT_2502=select e.pkey, e.name, a.name, e.locationkey from entity e, entity a where e.PKEY = %s and a.pkey = e.agentkey
ENTITY_V_SELECT_2503=select pkey FROM entity where typekey = %s and deleted = 0
ENTITY_V_SELECT_2504=select pkey FROM entity where typekey = %s and upper(name) LIKE upper('%%%s%%') and deleted = 0
ENTITY_V_SELECT_2505=select e.pkey, e.name, a.name, e.locationkey from entity e, entity a, entitytype et where e.deleted = 0 and a.deleted = 0 and et.name = '%s'
    + and e.typekey = et.pkey and a.PKEY = e.agentkey and upper(e.name) LIKE upper('%s')
ENTITY_V_SELECT_2506=select e.pkey, e.name, a.name, e.locationkey from entity e, entity a, entity p where e.deleted = 0 and a.deleted = 0 and p.deleted = 0 
    + and e.parentkey = p.pkey and upper(p.name) = upper('%s') and a.pkey = e.agentkey
ENTITY_V_SELECT_2507=select e.pkey, e.name, a.name, e.locationkey from entity e, entity a where e.deleted = 0 and a.deleted = 0 and e.parentkey = %s 
    + and a.pkey = e.agentkey
ENTITY_V_SELECT_2508=select e.pkey, e.name, a.name, e.locationkey from entity e, entity a, entity c where e.deleted = 0 and a.deleted = 0 and c.deleted = 0 
    + and c.parentkey = e.pkey and upper(c.name) = upper('%s') and a.pkey = e.agentkey
ENTITY_V_SELECT_2509=select e.pkey, e.name, a.name, e.locationkey from entity e, entity a, entity c where c.parentkey = e.pkey and c.pkey = %s 
    + and a.pkey = e.agentkey and e.deleted = 0 and a.deleted = 0 and c.deleted = 0 
ENTITY_V_SELECT_2510=select e.pkey, e.name, a.name, e.locationkey from entity e, entity a, entity p, entitytype et where e.deleted = 0 and a.deleted = 0 
    + and p.deleted = 0 and et.name = '%s' and p.typekey = et.pkey and e.parentkey = p.pkey and a.PKEY = e.agentkey
ENTITY_V_SELECT_2511=select e.pkey, e.name, a.name, e.locationkey from entity e, entity a, entity p, entitytype et where et.name = '%s' and p.typekey = et.pkey 
    + and e.parentkey = p.pkey and e.locationkey = %s  and a.PKEY = e.agentkey and e.deleted = 0 and a.deleted = 0 and p.deleted = 0 
ENTITY_V_SELECT_2512=select e.pkey, e.name, a.name, e.locationkey from entity e, entity a where e.deleted = 0 and a.deleted = 0 and upper(a.name) = upper('%s')
    + and e.agentkey = a.pkey and e.pkey <> a.pkey
ENTITY_V_SELECT_2513=select epv.value from entity e, entityparameter ep, entityparametervalue epv where e.deleted = 0 and upper(e.name) = upper('%s') and 
    + ep.NAME = '%s' and epv.parameterkey = ep.pkey and epv.ENTITYKEY = e.pkey
ENTITY_V_SELECT_2514=SELECT NAME, TYPEKEY, EP_DEFAULT FROM entityparameter
ENTITY_V_SELECT_2515=select pkey,name from entitytype where pkey <> 0
ENTITY_V_SELECT_2516=select PKEY from entity where NAME = '%s'
ENTITY_V_SELECT_2517=select name from entity where deleted = 0 and (PARENTKEY = %s or AGENTKEY = %s) and AGENTKEY <> PKEY
ENTITY_V_SELECT_2518=select pkey, name from entity where typekey in (select t.pkey from entitytype t, entitytypeparent p where t.pkey = p.et_parentkey and p.et_key = 
    + (select pkey from entitytype where name = '%s')) and deleted = 0
ENTITY_V_SELECT_2519=SELECT distinct e.AGENTNAME FROM entity_v e, entitytype et WHERE e.deleted = 0 and et.name ='%s' and et.pkey = e.typekey
ENTITY_V_SELECT_2520=SELECT distinct e.AGENTNAME FROM entity_v e, entitytype et WHERE e.deleted = 0 and et.name ='%s' and et.pkey = e.typekey and e.locationKey = %s
[[Oracle]]
ENTITY_V_SELECT_2551=SELECT e.TYPEKEY, e.NAME, e.ADDRESS, e.DESCRIPTION, e.SUBSYSTEMKEY, e.SUBSYSTEMNAME, e.PHYSICAL_SUBSYSTEM_KEY, e.PHYSICAL_SUBSYSTEM_NAME, 
    + e.LOCATIONKEY, e.LOCATIONNAME, e.SEREGI_ID, e.SEREGINAME, e.PARENTKEY, e.PARENTNAME, e.AGENTKEY, e.AGENTNAME, 
    + TO_CHAR(e.DATE_CREATED, 'YYYYMMDDHH24MISS') as DATE_CREATED, TO_CHAR(e.DATE_MODIFIED,'YYYYMMDDHH24MISS') as DATE_MODIFIED, e.pkey, 
    + et.name FROM entity_v e, entitytype et where upper(e.name) = upper('%s') and et.pkey = e.typekey and e.deleted = 0
ENTITY_V_SELECT_2552=SELECT e.TYPEKEY, e.NAME, e.ADDRESS, e.DESCRIPTION, e.SUBSYSTEMKEY, e.SUBSYSTEMNAME, PHYSICAL_SUBSYSTEM_KEY, e.PHYSICAL_SUBSYSTEM_NAME, 
    + e.LOCATIONKEY, e.LOCATIONNAME, e.SEREGI_ID, e.SEREGINAME, e.PARENTKEY, e.PARENTNAME, e.AGENTKEY, e.AGENTNAME,

    + entitytype et WHERE e.pkey = %s and et.pkey = e.typekey
ENTITY_V_SELECT_2553=SELECT e.TYPEKEY, e.NAME, e.ADDRESS, e.DESCRIPTION, e.SUBSYSTEMKEY, e.SUBSYSTEMNAME, e.PHYSICAL_SUBSYSTEM_KEY, e.PHYSICAL_SUBSYSTEM_NAME, 
    + e.LOCATIONKEY, e.LOCATIONNAME, e.SEREGI_ID, e.SEREGINAME, e.PARENTKEY, e.PARENTNAME, e.AGENTKEY, e.AGENTNAME, 
    + TO_CHAR(e.DATE_CREATED, 'YYYYMMDDHH24MISS'), TO_CHAR(e.DATE_MODIFIED, 'YYYYMMDDHH24MISS'), e.pkey, et.name FROM entity_v e,

ENTITY_V_SELECT_2554=SELECT e.TYPEKEY, e.NAME, e.ADDRESS, e.DESCRIPTION, e.SUBSYSTEMKEY, e.SUBSYSTEMNAME, e.PHYSICAL_SUBSYSTEM_KEY, e.PHYSICAL_SUBSYSTEM_NAME, 
    + e.LOCATIONKEY, e.LOCATIONNAME, e.SEREGI_ID, e.SEREGINAME, e.PARENTKEY, e.PARENTNAME, e.AGENTKEY, e.AGENTNAME, 
    + TO_CHAR(e.DATE_CREATED, 'YYYYMMDDHH24MISS'), TO_CHAR(e.DATE_MODIFIED, 'YYYYMMDDHH24MISS'), e.pkey, et.name FROM entity_v e, entitytype et 
    + WHERE et.name = '%s' and et.pkey = e.typekey and e.deleted = 0
ENTITY_V_SELECT_2555=SELECT e.TYPEKEY, e.NAME, e.ADDRESS, e.DESCRIPTION, e.SUBSYSTEMKEY, e.SUBSYSTEMNAME, PHYSICAL_SUBSYSTEM_KEY, PHYSICAL_SUBSYSTEM_NAME,
    + e.LOCATIONKEY, e.LOCATIONNAME, e.SEREGI_ID, e.SEREGINAME, e.PARENTKEY, e.PARENTNAME, e.AGENTKEY, e.AGENTNAME, 
    + TO_CHAR(e.DATE_CREATED, 'YYYYMMDDHH24MISS'), TO_CHAR(e.DATE_MODIFIED, 'YYYYMMDDHH24MISS'), e.pkey, et.name FROM entity_v e, entitytype et
    + WHERE e.deleted = 0 and et.name = '%s'  and et.pkey = e.typekey and e.locationKey = %s  and upper(e.name) LIKE upper('%s')
ENTITY_V_SELECT_2556=SELECT e.TYPEKEY, e.NAME, e.ADDRESS, e.DESCRIPTION, e.SUBSYSTEMKEY, e.SUBSYSTEMNAME, PHYSICAL_SUBSYSTEM_KEY, PHYSICAL_SUBSYSTEM_NAME, 
    + e.LOCATIONKEY, e.LOCATIONNAME, e.SEREGI_ID, e.SEREGINAME, e.PARENTKEY, e.PARENTNAME, e.AGENTKEY, e.AGENTNAME, 
    + TO_CHAR(e.DATE_CREATED, 'YYYYMMDDHH24MISS'), TO_CHAR(e.DATE_MODIFIED, 'YYYYMMDDHH24MISS'), e.pkey, et.name FROM entity_v e, entitytype et
    + WHERE e.deleted = 0 and et.name = '%s' and et.pkey = e.typekey %s
ENTITY_V_SELECT_2557=SELECT e.TYPEKEY, e.NAME, e.ADDRESS, e.DESCRIPTION, e.SUBSYSTEMKEY, e.SUBSYSTEMNAME, e.PHYSICAL_SUBSYSTEM_KEY, e.PHYSICAL_SUBSYSTEM_NAME,
    + e.LOCATIONKEY, e.LOCATIONNAME, e.SEREGI_ID, e.SEREGINAME, e.PARENTKEY, e.PARENTNAME, e.AGENTKEY, e.AGENTNAME, 
    + TO_CHAR(e.DATE_CREATED, 'YYYYMMDDHH24MISS'), TO_CHAR(e.DATE_MODIFIED, 'YYYYMMDDHH24MISS'), e.pkey, ec.name FROM entity_v e, entity_v p, 
    + entitytype et, entitytype ec WHERE e.deleted = 0 and e.PARENTKEY = p.pkey and ec.PKEY = e.TYPEKEY and (p.deleted=0 and p.typekey =

     + FROM ENTITY_V 
     + WHERE NAME LIKE '%s.TIS.%%.%%.%%' 
     + AND NAME NOT LIKE '%s.TIS.STIS.%%.%%' 
     + AND NAME NOT LIKE '%s.TIS.ISCS.%%.%%'
     + AND TYPEKEY = (SELECT PKEY  FROM ENTITYTYPE  WHERE NAME = '%s')
ENTITY_V_SELECT_2531=SELECT UNIQUE (SUBSTR(NAME, 1, INSTR(NAME, '.', 1, 1)) || (SUBSTR(NAME, INSTR(NAME, '.', 1, 2) + 1, 
     + INSTR(NAME, '.', -1, 1)-INSTR(NAME, '.', 1, 2) -1 ))) AS NAME 
     + FROM ENTITY_V 
     + WHERE NAME LIKE '%s.TIS.%%.%%.%%' 
     + AND NAME NOT LIKE '%s.TIS.STIS.%%.%%' 
     + AND NAME NOT LIKE '%s.TIS.ISCS.%%.%%' 
     + AND TYPEKEY = (SELECT PKEY  FROM ENTITYTYPE  WHERE NAME = '%s')

     + me_message_type.type_name from event,me_message_type where sessionkey = '%s' and (( eventtype=(select memtyp_id from me_message_type where type_name='%s')) or ( eventtype=(select memtyp_id from me_message_type where type_name='%s'))
     + or ( eventtype=(select memtyp_id from me_message_type where type_name='%s')) or ( eventtype=(select memtyp_id from me_message_type where type_name='%s'))) and event.eventtype = me_message_type.memtyp_id

     + mt.type_name as TypeName, ent.name as EntityName, op.name, sev.name, subsys.name as SubsystemName, loc.name as LocationName, e.ASSET_NAME from event e,me_message_type mt, entity ent, location loc, subsystem subsys,
     + ta_session s right join event et on s.pkey = et.sessionkey left join operator op on s.operatorkey = op.pkey,alarm a right join event ett on a.alarm_id = ett.alarm_id left join alarmseverity sev on a.severity = sev.pkey
     + where e.entitykey = ent.pkey AND mt.memtyp_id = e.eventtype and e.pkey = et.pkey and e.pkey = ett.pkey and et.pkey = ett.pkey AND ent.locationkey = loc.pkey AND ent.SUBSYSTEMKEY = subsys.PKEY and %s %s

     + ep.typekey = (select pkey from entitytype where name = '%s')

     + entityparameter ep, entityparameterdatatype epdt where ep.typekey = (select pkey from entitytype where name = '%s') and epdt.pkey = ep.ep_default_datatype

     + entityparameter ep, entityparametervalue ev, entityparameterdatatype epdt where ep.typekey = (select pkey from entitytype where name = '%s') and ep.pkey = ev.parameterkey and ev.entitykey = %s 
     + and epdt.pkey = ep.ep_default_datatype union select ep.name, nvl(ep.ep_default_datatype, 0), '' as value, ep.ep_default,ep.visible, ep.ep_mandatory, ep.onlineupdate, epdt.datatype, ep_validation from
     + entityparameter ep, entity e, entityparameterdatatype epdt where e.deleted = 0 and ep.typekey = e.typekey and e.pkey = %s and ep.name not in ( select ep.name from entityparameter ep, 
     + entityparametervalue ev where ep.typekey = (select pkey from entitytype where name = '%s') and ep.pkey = ev.parameterkey and ev.entitykey = %s) and epdt.pkey = ep.ep_default_datatype

RA_SUBSCRIBERS_SELECT_34551=select unique GROUP_RASUBS_ID,RASUBS.SUBSCRIBER_NAME,RASUBS.SUBSCRIBER_TYPE,RASUBS.LOCATION,nvl(RASUBS.LOCATION_KEY,0) as LOCATION_KEY from RA_GROUP_MEMBERS RAGMEM inner join ra_subscribers RASUBS on (GROUP_RASUBS_ID = RASUBS_ID)
RA_SUBSCRIBERS_SELECT_34552=select 0 AS RAGMEM_ID,GROUP_RASUBS_ID AS RASUBS_ID, G.SUBSCRIBER_NAME,G.SUBSCRIBER_TYPE,G.LOCATION,nvl(G.LOCATION_KEY,0) as LOCATION_KEY from ra_group_members ragmem inner join ra_subscribers G ON (GROUP_RASUBS_ID = RASUBS_ID)
     + where ragmem.GROUP_RASUBS_ID = '%s' union select RAGMEM_ID,M.RASUBS_ID,M.SUBSCRIBER_NAME,M.SUBSCRIBER_TYPE, M.LOCATION,nvl(M.LOCATION_KEY,0) as LOCATION_KEY from ra_group_members ragmem inner join ra_subscribers   M
     + ON (MEMBER_RASUBS_ID = RASUBS_ID) where ragmem.GROUP_RASUBS_ID = '%s' order by RAGMEM_ID

IN_INCIDENT_REPORT_SELECT_52551=select inc.ININCI_ID,TO_CHAR(inc.CREATE_DATE,'YYYYMMDDHH24MISS'),inc.TITLE,loc1.NAME,loc2.NAME,INNER_TRACK,OUTER_TRACK,TRAIN_ID,ALARM_ID,asset.NAME,SUBSYSTEM.NAME,
     + cre.NAME,creprof.NAME,TO_CHAR(CLOSE_DATE,'YYYYMMDDHH24MISS'),inc.ENTITY_ID from in_incident_report inc, location loc1, location loc2,ENTITY asset, OPERATOR cre, 
     + se_profile creprof, SUBSYSTEM  where inc.LOCATI_ID_1 = loc1.PKEY (+) AND inc.LOCATI_ID_2 = loc2.PKEY (+) AND inc.CREATE_OPERAT_ID = cre.PKEY (+) 
     + AND inc.CREATE_SEPROF_ID = creprof.SEPROF_ID (+) AND inc.ENTITY_ID = asset.PKEY (+) AND asset.SUBSYSTEMKEY = SUBSYSTEM.PKEY (+)
IN_INCIDENT_REPORT_SELECT_52552=select inc.TITLE,inc.CREATE_OPERAT_ID,inc.CREATE_SEPROF_ID,TO_CHAR(inc.CREATE_DATE,'YYYYMMDDHH24MISS'),NVL(inc.MODIFY_OPERAT_ID,0) as MODIFY_OPERAT_ID ,
     + NVL(inc.MODIFY_SEPROF_ID,0) as MODIFY_SEPROF_ID ,TO_CHAR(inc.MODIFY_DATE,'YYYYMMDDHH24MISS'),inc.FALSE_INCIDENT,NVL(inc.ENTITY_ID,0) as ENTITY_ID,
     + inc.LOCATI_ID_1,inc.LOCATI_ID_2,loc1.NAME,loc2.NAME,inc.TRAIN_ID,TO_CHAR(nvl(inc.START_DATE,TO_DATE('12:00:00 01/01/1990','hh:mi:ss dd/mm/yyyy')),'YYYYMMDDHH24MISS'),
     + TO_CHAR(nvl(inc.END_DATE,TO_DATE('12:00:00 01/01/1990','hh:mi:ss dd/mm/yyyy')),'YYYYMMDDHH24MISS'),inc.INNER_TRACK,inc.OUTER_TRACK,NVL(inc.KM_LOSS,0) as KM_LOSS,
     + NVL(inc.INITIAL_DELAY,0) as INITIAL_DELAY,NVL(inc.TOTAL_DELAY,0) as TOTAL_DELAY,inc.ALARM_ID,inc.ALARM_DESC,inc.ALARM_VALUE,inc.OPERATORS,inc.COMMENTS,inc.RECOMMENDATION,
     + inc.INSTAT_ID,TO_CHAR(nvl(inc.CLOSE_DATE,TO_DATE('12:00:00 01/01/1990','hh:mi:ss dd/mm/yyyy')),'YYYYMMDDHH24MISS'),inc.CREATE_LOCATI_ID from in_incident_report inc, 
     + location loc1, location loc2 where inc.ININCI_ID = '%s' AND inc.LOCATI_ID_1 = loc1.PKEY (+) AND inc.LOCATI_ID_2 = loc2.PKEY (+)

     + INSTAT_ID,CLOSE_DATE,EDIT_OPERATOR_COUNT,CREATE_LOCATI_ID) values (''%s'',''%s'',%s,%s,%s,NULL,NULL,NULL,%s,%s,''%s'',''%s'',''%s'',%s,%s,%s,%s,%s,%s,%s,''%s'',''%s'',''%s'',''%s'',''%s'',''%s'',''%s'',NULL,1,%s)')

[[MySQL]]
IN_INCIDENT_REPORT_SELECT_52551=select inc.ININCI_ID,DATE_FORMAT(inc.CREATE_DATE,'%Y%m%d%H%i%S'),inc.TITLE,loc1.NAME, loc2.NAME,inc.INNER_TRACK,inc.OUTER_TRACK,inc.TRAIN_ID,inc.ALARM_ID,asset.NAME,
     + sub.NAME,cre.NAME,creprof.NAME,DATE_FORMAT(inc.CLOSE_DATE,'%Y%m%d%H%i%S'),inc.ENTITY_ID from in_incident_report inc left join location loc1 on inc.LOCATI_ID_1 = loc1.PKEY 
     + left join location loc2 on inc.LOCATI_ID_2 = loc2.PKEY left join operator cre on inc.CREATE_OPERAT_ID = cre.PKEY left join  se_profile creprof on inc.CREATE_SEPROF_ID = creprof.SEPROF_ID
     + left join entity asset on inc.ENTITY_ID = asset.PKEY left join subsystem sub on sub.pkey = asset.subsystemkey
IN_INCIDENT_REPORT_SELECT_52552=select inc.TITLE,inc.CREATE_OPERAT_ID,inc.CREATE_SEPROF_ID,DATE_FORMAT(inc.CREATE_DATE,'%%Y%%m%%d%%H%%i%%S'),IF(inc.MODIFY_OPERAT_ID IS NULL,0,inc.MODIFY_OPERAT_ID) as MODIFY_OPERAT_ID,
     + IF(inc.MODIFY_SEPROF_ID IS NULL,0,inc.MODIFY_SEPROF_ID) as MODIFY_SEPROF_ID ,DATE_FORMAT(inc.MODIFY_DATE,'%%Y%%m%%d%%H%%i%%S'),inc.FALSE_INCIDENT,IF(inc.ENTITY_ID IS NULL,0,inc.ENTITY_ID) as ENTITY_ID,
     + inc.LOCATI_ID_1,inc.LOCATI_ID_2,loc1.NAME,loc2.NAME,inc.TRAIN_ID,DATE_FORMAT(IF(inc.START_DATE IS NULL,STR_TO_DATE('12:00:00 01/01/1990','%%H:%%i:%%S %%d/%%m/%%Y'),inc.START_DATE),'%%Y%%m%%d%%H%%i%%S'),
     + DATE_FORMAT(IF(inc.END_DATE IS NULL,STR_TO_DATE('12:00:00 01/01/1990','%%H:%%i:%%S %%d/%%m/%%Y'),inc.END_DATE),'%%Y%%m%%d%%H%%i%%S'),inc.INNER_TRACK,inc.OUTER_TRACK,IF(inc.KM_LOSS IS NULL,0,inc.KM_LOSS) as KM_LOSS,
     + IF(inc.INITIAL_DELAY IS NULL,0,inc.INITIAL_DELAY) as INITIAL_DELAY,IF(inc.TOTAL_DELAY IS NULL,0,inc.TOTAL_DELAY) as TOTAL_DELAY,inc.ALARM_ID,inc.ALARM_DESC,inc.ALARM_VALUE,inc.OPERATORS,inc.COMMENTS,
     + inc.RECOMMENDATION,inc.INSTAT_ID,DATE_FORMAT(IF(inc.CLOSE_DATE IS NULL,STR_TO_DATE('12:00:00 01/01/1990','%%H:%%i:%%S %%d/%%m/%%Y'),inc.CLOSE_DATE),'%%Y%%m%%d%%H%%i%%S'),inc.CREATE_LOCATI_ID from in_incident_report inc
     + left join location loc2 on inc.LOCATI_ID_2 = loc2.PKEY left join location loc1 on inc.LOCATI_ID_1 = loc1.PKEY where inc.ININCI_ID = '%s'

STEP_DETAILES_SELECT_63552=select step_details.p_key, step_details.position, step_details.name,step_type.type_value, if(step_details.description is null or step_details.description = '', '%s', step_details.description),step_details.skip, step_details.skippable, step_details.delay,
     + if(step_details.ignore_failure is null, 0, step_details.ignore_failure), if(step_details.no_wait is null, 0, step_details.no_wait) from step_details, node_tree, step_type where step_details.fk_node_tree = node_tree.p_key 
     + and step_details.fk_step_type = step_type.p_key and step_details.fk_node_tree = %s %s order by step_details.position
